Chapter Summary

This is just a short one! I'll be updating pretty regularly but it'll probably be a few chapters until I find an upload schedule that works!

Chapter 9: The Red Room

Chapter Notes

Surprise! Two chapters in a day!

Also, I just wanted to thank everyone for leaving such nice comments! Like I said at the start, I haven’t written in years and now that I’ve started I’m realising how much I missed it!

I’m pretty sure I’m going to have to raise the chapter count again soon but I’m uploading pretty much daily! ☺️

See the end of the chapter for more notes

Rio jogs down the aisle towards the safe and crouches.

“Can you even wait to see the look on that smug assholes face, Jen?” Rio grins as she starts to dial in the code.

It isn’t until she opens the safe door, reaches in and pulls out the small box in the centre that she realizes Jen hasn’t answered her. Had she left her outside?

“Jen?”

She turns to look back down the aisle towards the door and doesn’t see Jen.

But she does see Agatha.

On one knee right in front of her at the bottom of the step.

“A-Agatha what are you-“

“Open the box.” She whispers in reply.

Rio looks down to the little black box in her hand and flicks it open.

A beautiful green jewel glitters atop a ring dead centre of the box.

“A-are you-“

“I know you said that if we ever were to…” Agatha anxiously clears her throat. Rio notices that she is incredibly nervous. She reaches for the box, turns it and pulls out the ring. “…if we were to do this it would be when I tell you I want it. Because I’ve already done this before.”

Rio stares down at her dumbly, in complete shock at what the hell is happening.

“But Rio I haven’t done this before. I haven’t promised to spend my life with someone I love so completely before. I haven’t been so sure of anything before I met you.” Her eyes are watery.

“A-and I know you don’t want a big wedding.” She says quickly. “God knows I don’t either, but if you-“

“Yes.” Rio blurts. “Jesus, did you think I’d say anything other than yes!?” She laughs tearfully as she steps down and kisses Agatha, both smiling, their cheeks wet as their tears mix.

 

“Mama, Mama! Did you say yes!?”

“Nicky, no!” Alice calls out, racing towards the three year old that’s hurtling himself down the aisle towards them both. “I’m so sorry Agatha, I tried to hold him back but-“

Rio looks over Agatha’s shoulder to see her son beaming up at them widely wearing a little suit.

“Baby! What are you doing here I thought you were supposed to be at the movies with your Grandpa today!” She opens her arms and Nicky comes barreling into her at speed.

“He is with Grandpa!” John steps out of the back room and walks down to the pedestal in front of the three of them. “But I’m afraid we all told you a little lie this morning, Rio! Agains my nature, of course, but worth it, hope you’ll agree.”

John is dressed as if at work, clothed in the same outfit he wears to sermons.

“W-what are you…”

Jen, Alice, Lilia, Wanda, Kate and a few others from town start piling into the room. Agatha shifts nervously in front of her.

“So I know you said you’d like something small…and you also said that the stress of planning a wedding might kill you, so I took a really risky gamble and-“

“Agatha…” realization finally dawns on Rio. “Are we getting married right now?”

Her eyes are bugging out of her head.

“Uhm…if you want to?” Agatha says almost bashfully. “No pressure! Because if you don’t, I’m sure John could play this off into a sermon or some-“

Rio pulls Agatha back in to kiss her. She feels Agatha melt in relief against her. Nicky giggles next to them which reminds Rio of his presence and she pulls away.

“I’m the teddy bear!” Nicky grins his adorable little gap-toothed smile, presenting two wedding bands proudly from his pocket.

“Ring bearer, baby.” Agatha laughs. “And you’ll need to hold on to them until Grandpa asks for ‘em, okay?”

Nicky looks a little worried for a second.

“Don’t worry buddy! You’re doing great!” John shoots him a wink.

“So, Rio, what do you say? Ready to get married?” John asks with a smirk.

 

 

Rio and her wife sit at their table at the back of the decked out community centre that evidently has been set up during the scavenger hunt this morning. Nicky is currently dancing with his Aunties to baby shark on the dance floor and having the time of his life up past bedtime.

“God he’s so you.” Agatha laughs fondly as her hand rests atop Rios, rubbing gently.

“He’s so us.” Rio smiles, watching Nicky directing Alice on how to do the grandma shark action correctly. “Did you really send me on a hunt across town to keep me busy to set all of this up?”

Agatha smiles.

“Sure did. Good pay off though.” She winks.

“I love you so much for the sweetest proposal ever, but I love you even more for the fact that you planned this in such a way that I never had to plan a wedding.”

Agatha laughs.

“So now I get to reap the rewards tonight, right?” She lowers her voice and leans in closer.

“Think you’re forgetting about our three-year-old boss who’s got us working nights at random recently.” Rio whispers back.

“Oh, I didn’t mention? His aunties are keeping him tonight.”

“Oh really?” Rios voice drops suggestively.

“Yeah. And I believe I won a bet today?” Agatha grins at her as her eyebrows furrow.

“Uhm…no? I won the bet. I got to the safe-“

“Where I put the rings because I was already there.” Agatha grins smugly.

“But that’s not-“

“You agreed. If I got there first, you’d let me be the last audio on your profile.” She smirks. “I can’t see any better timing than tonight. Nicky’s with Jen and Alice, so we can be as loud as we want.”

Rios eyes darken.

“We could…”

“That a yes?”

“Yes.” Rio swallows “It’s most definitely a yes”

Agatha lights up.

 

“In the guesthouse? For old times sake?”

 

“You know something? Let’s just go home now. I’m sure no one will miss us.” Rio whispers desperately.

 

Agatha chuckles.

 

”And risk being rude to our guests?” She feigns horror.

 

”It’s that or we’re about to revisit that church and I don’t think the acoustics in there will be nearly as good for recording-“ 

Agatha shoots up from her seat, dragging Rio by her wrist.

 

”Point made. Let’s go home.”
